 - atah tamaam tarah kii sanchari bimariyon kaa khatra bad jaataa he
 - Water usage should be increased during this month and oily things should be eaten at least
 - jahaan tak sambhav ho sattu or rasadaar falon kaa prayog karnaa chahie
 - And avoid sleeping till late
